    [Project1].[Name] AS [Name]

        [Extent1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
        [Extent1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
        [Extent1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
        [Extent1].[Login] AS [Login], 
        [Extent1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
        [Extent1].[About] AS [About], 
        [Extent1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
        [Extent1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
        [Extent1].[Email] AS [Email], 
        [Extent1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
        [Extent1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp],

        [Extent1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
        [Extent1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Category_Id] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM  [dbo].[AspNetUsers] AS [Extent1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[Category_Id] AS [Category_Id], [Extent2].[ApplicationUser_Id] AS [ApplicationUser_Id], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name]
            FROM  [dbo].[CategoryApplicationUsers] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[Categories] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[Category_Id] ) AS [Join1] ON [Extent1].[Id] = [Join1].[ApplicationUser_Id]
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[Id] ASC, [Project1].[C1] ASC

SELECT TOP (1) 
    [Project1].[C1] AS [C1], 
    [Project1].[MigrationId] AS [MigrationId], 
    [Project1].[Model] AS [Model], 
    [Project1].[ProductVersion] AS [ProductVersion]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Extent1].[MigrationId] AS [MigrationId], 
        [Extent1].[Model] AS [Model], 
        [Extent1].[ProductVersion] AS [ProductVersion], 
        1 AS [C1]
        FROM [dbo].[__MigrationHistory] AS [Extent1]
        WHERE [Extent1].[ContextKey] = @p__linq__0
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[MigrationId] DESC

    [Project1].[About] AS [About], 
    [Project1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
    [Project1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
    [Project1].[Email] AS [Email], 
    [Project1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
    [Project1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
    [Project1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
    [Project1].[C1] AS [C1], 
    [Project1].[Id1] AS [Id1], 
    [Project1].[Name] AS [Name]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Extent1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
        [Extent1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
        [Extent1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
        [Extent1].[Login] AS [Login], 
        [Extent1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
        [Extent1].[About] AS [About], 
        [Extent1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
        [Extent1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
        [Extent1].[Email] AS [Email], 
        [Extent1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
        [Extent1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
        [Extent1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Category_Id] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM  [dbo].[AspNetUsers] AS [Extent1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[Category_Id] AS [Category_Id], [Extent2].[ApplicationUser_Id] AS [ApplicationUser_Id], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name]
            FROM  [dbo].[CategoryApplicationUsers] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[Categories] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[Category_Id] ) AS [Join1] ON [Extent1].[Id] = [Join1].[ApplicationUser_Id]
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[Id] ASC, [Project1].[C1] ASC

SELECT 
    [Project1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
    [Project1].[Id] AS [Id], 
    [Project1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
    [Project1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
    [Project1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
    [Project1].[Login] AS [Login], 
    [Project1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
    [Project1].[About] AS [About], 
    [Project1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
    [Project1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
    [Project1].[Email] AS [Email], 
    [Project1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
    [Project1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
    [Project1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
    [Project1].[C1] AS [C1], 
    [Project1].[Id1] AS [Id1], 
    [Project1].[Name] AS [Name]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Extent1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
        [Extent1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
        [Extent1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
        [Extent1].[Login] AS [Login], 
        [Extent1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
        [Extent1].[About] AS [About], 
        [Extent1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
        [Extent1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
        [Extent1].[Email] AS [Email], 
        [Extent1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
        [Extent1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
        [Extent1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Category_Id] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM  [dbo].[AspNetUsers] AS [Extent1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[Category_Id] AS [Category_Id], [Extent2].[ApplicationUser_Id] AS [ApplicationUser_Id], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name]
            FROM  [dbo].[CategoryApplicationUsers] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[Categories] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[Category_Id] ) AS [Join1] ON [Extent1].[Id] = [Join1].[ApplicationUser_Id]
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[Id] ASC, [Project1].[C1] ASC

SELECT 
    [Project1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
    [Project1].[Id] AS [Id], 
    [Project1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
    [Project1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
    [Project1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
    [Project1].[Login] AS [Login], 
    [Project1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
    [Project1].[About] AS [About], 
    [Project1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
    [Project1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
    [Project1].[Email] AS [Email], 
    [Project1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
    [Project1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
    [Project1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
    [Project1].[C1] AS [C1], 
    [Project1].[Id1] AS [Id1], 
    [Project1].[Name] AS [Name]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Extent1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
        [Extent1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
        [Extent1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
        [Extent1].[Login] AS [Login], 
        [Extent1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
        [Extent1].[About] AS [About], 
        [Extent1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
        [Extent1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
        [Extent1].[Email] AS [Email], 
        [Extent1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
        [Extent1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
        [Extent1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Category_Id] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM  [dbo].[AspNetUsers] AS [Extent1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[Category_Id] AS [Category_Id], [Extent2].[ApplicationUser_Id] AS [ApplicationUser_Id], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name]
            FROM  [dbo].[CategoryApplicationUsers] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[Categories] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[Category_Id] ) AS [Join1] ON [Extent1].[Id] = [Join1].[ApplicationUser_Id]
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[Id] ASC, [Project1].[C1] ASC

    [Project1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
    [Project1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
    [Project1].[C1] AS [C1], 
    [Project1].[Id1] AS [Id1], 
    [Project1].[Name] AS [Name]

        [Extent1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
        [Extent1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
        [Extent1].[Login] AS [Login], 
        [Extent1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
        [Extent1].[About] AS [About], 
        [Extent1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
        [Extent1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
        [Extent1].[Email] AS [Email],

        [Extent1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
        [Extent1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Category_Id] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM  [dbo].[AspNetUsers] AS [Extent1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[Category_Id] AS [Category_Id], [Extent2].[ApplicationUser_Id] AS [ApplicationUser_Id], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name]
            FROM  [dbo].[CategoryApplicationUsers] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[Categories] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[Category_Id] ) AS [Join1] ON [Extent1].[Id] = [Join1].[ApplicationUser_Id]
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[Id] ASC, [Project1].[C1] ASC

SELECT 
    [Project1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
    [Project1].[Id] AS [Id], 
    [Project1].[FullName] AS [FullName], 
    [Project1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
    [Project1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
    [Project1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
    [Project1].[Login] AS [Login], 
    [Project1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
    [Project1].[About] AS [About], 
    [Project1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
    [Project1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
    [Project1].[Email] AS [Email], 
    [Project1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
    [Project1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
    [Project1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
    [Project1].[C1] AS [C1], 
    [Project1].[Id1] AS [Id1], 
    [Project1].[Name] AS [Name]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Extent1].[FullName] AS [FullName], 
        [Extent1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
        [Extent1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
        [Extent1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
        [Extent1].[Login] AS [Login], 
        [Extent1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
        [Extent1].[About] AS [About], 
        [Extent1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
        [Extent1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
        [Extent1].[Email] AS [Email], 
        [Extent1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
        [Extent1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
        [Extent1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Category_Id] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM  [dbo].[AspNetUsers] AS [Extent1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[Category_Id] AS [Category_Id], [Extent2].[ApplicationUser_Id] AS [ApplicationUser_Id], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name]
            FROM  [dbo].[CategoryApplicationUsers] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[Categories] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[Category_Id] ) AS [Join1] ON [Extent1].[Id] = [Join1].[ApplicationUser_Id]
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[Id] ASC, [Project1].[C1] ASC
-- Executing at 13.03.2018 21:57:03 +02:00
-- Completed in 1 ms with result: SqlDataReader

Closed connection at 13.03.2018 21:57:03 +02:00
Opened connection at 13.03.2018 21:57:03 +02:00

SELECT 
    [Project1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
    [Project1].[Id] AS [Id], 
    [Project1].[FullName] AS [FullName], 
    [Project1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
    [Project1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
    [Project1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
    [Project1].[Login] AS [Login], 
    [Project1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
    [Project1].[About] AS [About], 
    [Project1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
    [Project1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
    [Project1].[Email] AS [Email], 
    [Project1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
    [Project1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
    [Project1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
    [Project1].[C1] AS [C1], 
    [Project1].[Id1] AS [Id1], 
    [Project1].[Name] AS [Name]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Extent1].[FullName] AS [FullName], 
        [Extent1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
        [Extent1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
        [Extent1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
        [Extent1].[Login] AS [Login], 
        [Extent1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
        [Extent1].[About] AS [About], 
        [Extent1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
        [Extent1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
        [Extent1].[Email] AS [Email], 
        [Extent1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
        [Extent1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
        [Extent1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Category_Id] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM  [dbo].[AspNetUsers] AS [Extent1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[Category_Id] AS [Category_Id], [Extent2].[ApplicationUser_Id] AS [ApplicationUser_Id], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name]
            FROM  [dbo].[CategoryApplicationUsers] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[Categories] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[Category_Id] ) AS [Join1] ON [Extent1].[Id] = [Join1].[ApplicationUser_Id]
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[Id] ASC, [Project1].[C1] ASC

SELECT 
    [Project1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
    [Project1].[Id] AS [Id], 
    [Project1].[FullName] AS [FullName], 
    [Project1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
    [Project1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
    [Project1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
    [Project1].[Login] AS [Login], 
    [Project1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
    [Project1].[About] AS [About], 
    [Project1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
    [Project1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
    [Project1].[Email] AS [Email], 
    [Project1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
    [Project1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
    [Project1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
    [Project1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
    [Project1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
    [Project1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
    [Project1].[C1] AS [C1], 
    [Project1].[Id1] AS [Id1], 
    [Project1].[Name] AS [Name]
    FROM ( SELECT 
        [Extent1].[Id] AS [Id], 
        [Extent1].[FullName] AS [FullName], 
        [Extent1].[Firstname] AS [Firstname], 
        [Extent1].[Lastname] AS [Lastname], 
        [Extent1].[BirthDate] AS [BirthDate], 
        [Extent1].[Login] AS [Login], 
        [Extent1].[AvatarImage] AS [AvatarImage], 
        [Extent1].[About] AS [About], 
        [Extent1].[CityId] AS [CityId], 
        [Extent1].[RegistrationDate] AS [RegistrationDate], 
        [Extent1].[Email] AS [Email], 
        [Extent1].[EmailConfirmed] AS [EmailConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[PasswordHash] AS [PasswordHash], 
        [Extent1].[SecurityStamp] AS [SecurityStamp], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumber] AS [PhoneNumber], 
        [Extent1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed] AS [PhoneNumberConfirmed], 
        [Extent1].[TwoFactorEnabled] AS [TwoFactorEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEndDateUtc] AS [LockoutEndDateUtc], 
        [Extent1].[LockoutEnabled] AS [LockoutEnabled], 
        [Extent1].[AccessFailedCount] AS [AccessFailedCount], 
        [Extent1].[UserName] AS [UserName], 
        [Join1].[Id] AS [Id1], 
        [Join1].[Name] AS [Name], 
        CASE WHEN ([Join1].[Category_Id] IS NULL) THEN CAST(NULL AS int) ELSE 1 END AS [C1]
        FROM  [dbo].[AspNetUsers] AS [Extent1]
        LEFT OUTER JOIN  (SELECT [Extent2].[Category_Id] AS [Category_Id], [Extent2].[ApplicationUser_Id] AS [ApplicationUser_Id], [Extent3].[Id] AS [Id], [Extent3].[Name] AS [Name]
            FROM  [dbo].[CategoryApplicationUsers] AS [Extent2]
            INNER JOIN [dbo].[Categories] AS [Extent3] ON [Extent3].[Id] = [Extent2].[Category_Id] ) AS [Join1] ON [Extent1].[Id] = [Join1].[ApplicationUser_Id]
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[Id] ASC, [Project1].[C1] ASC
-- Executing at 13.03.2018 22:11:58 +02:00
-- Completed in 21 ms with result: SqlDataReader

Closed connection at 13.03.2018 22:11:58 +02:00
Opened connection at 13.03.2018 22:11:58 +02:00
